function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

// File added: plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html') && (sha1_file('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/contoso_example_ltd/index.html');
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql') != '3531147e51dc46fa6f26f266680f27cf4f0b7b58') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql') !== '3531147e51dc46fa6f26f266680f27cf4f0b7b58') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql') !== 'a2c76e6fd6c4795bf0d71f3a381991b556b02598') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql') !== '3531147e51dc46fa6f26f266680f27cf4f0b7b58') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_access.sql');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql') !== '611ef636669f5d58aff1a91f143c25478cfc19fe') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql') !== 'd742a20c69e2e19adefa97f77d6d71eca7fe31ee') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql') !== '611ef636669f5d58aff1a91f143c25478cfc19fe') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_mssql.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql') != 'a85910665b0b55651c33249cde6f16d3ef778d7d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql') !== 'a85910665b0b55651c33249cde6f16d3ef778d7d') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql') !== 'ba30a5a4d5dfc95eaff1006ab35ac98d361e5ed5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql') !== 'a85910665b0b55651c33249cde6f16d3ef778d7d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_mysql.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql') != 'b26c011e580b0cc2f1b725e95c7367622e6c6ca7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql') !== 'b26c011e580b0cc2f1b725e95c7367622e6c6ca7') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql') !== 'e08790f4c3e9b128390167cd05ef2cc23f6f61f3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql') !== 'b26c011e580b0cc2f1b725e95c7367622e6c6ca7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_pgsql.sql');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql') != '8436807a2a5b6eab27f9f73f8b806e33219106f5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql') !== '8436807a2a5b6eab27f9f73f8b806e33219106f5') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql') !== '8436807a2a5b6eab27f9f73f8b806e33219106f5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_country_sqlite.sql');
		}
	}
